\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Represents an unstructured piece of information, about an entity found in the sources.

\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2fortranscanner_8l_a4481d3eae9a04af883d868f23c4cbffc}{parse\+Main()}} in scanner.\+l will generate a tree of these entries. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2entry_8h_source_l00061}{61}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2src_2entry_8h_source}{entry.\+h}}.
